< Text>
I have brought in various devices, including a MacBook Pro, an iPad and an iPhone, for diagnosis and repair to Computerland over the last TEN years.

Every time, I received very professional, knowledgeable, fast and friendly service for all issues (such as upgrading to a SSD, installing the latest iOS, replacing a waterlogged track pad, troubleshooting/fixing a virus-infested tablet, or restoring a phone that was stuck in the middle of a software upgrade).

Had an amazing night, was greeted at least four times just on the way to our table. Their process is a little different from normal restaurants so we were patiently taught how they work and before we knew it, we were being offered selections from vegetables to salads to filet mignon to lamb to chicken to so many different varieties you couldn't imagine. It's almost literally a reverse buffet, and then to top it all off the tres leche cake was oh my God so gloriously delicious. Reasonable price for all you can eat filet mignon, I swear, they were offering us helpings so fast that before we could stop or knew what was happening we were so stuffed we could hardly breathe. Would recommend a hundred times over, exceptional service, food and prices.<//review>

<UserId.>116192558503984201933</UserId.><Name>Suzette C.<//Name><Date>1559326572878<//Date><Rating>5<//Rating><Text>In this day and age there are a tremendous amount of options for one to dine at. I have barely tried all of the world's cuisine, but I intend to one bite at a time. A Brazilian steakhouse happens to be one of them!

On A Saturday evening we had reservations for 6:00 pm.  By then the parking lot was completely full and we had to use Napa Winery Inn's lot next door. No big deal. We were politely greeted and waited a few minutes before being seated.

For attire you can get away with everyday wear. Not everyone followed this, but to my surprise there were a lot of guests dressed casually. I felt a little overdressed from everyone. Nonetheless a lot of the staff had smiles no matter who they were serving.

Our waitress Tahis for the evening was just wonderful from beginning to end. Maybe I just haven't been to many restaurants with excellent service. It was the little things she did on her own like asking if we wanted fresh mashed potatoes or bananas throughout our meal. Without asking she gave us new plates instead of using the same one. Her demeanor was genuinely hospitable and very attentive. She alone gets five stars!

Buffet ($59.95)-

They do have a gourmet salad bar that had a variety of items including; vegetables, cured meats, cheeses, sushi, deviled eggs, bacon, and more. There were also a few selections of hot soups. We were also given cheese bread and mashed potatoes at our table.  I will admit, nothing was really memorable compared to the meats we had. Although, I would like to try the soups next time though.

From a handful of mixed reviews I was hesitant to how our experience would be with the all you can eat meats. On a whole we happily devoured each delicious mouthful of seasoned well meat. The bottom sirloin steak was the only tidbit that I thought was unpleasantly overcooked. Sidenote, the simple caramelized bananas went perfect with the meat. The sweet and savory hit the spot!

For the amount you pay per person it is expensive and probably not the best place to bring children unless they really have an appetite. I would suggest eating your money's worth before calling it quits! Our lovely dining experience was exactly what we needed to celebrate our 11 year anniversary. My Love is already set on having our anniversary dinner there again!<//Text>< Pictures>

< review>
This place was easy to find and absolutely gorgeous inside! I came with my best friend to celebrate her birthday, which I mentioned in the reservation, and they were great about it! They bring a ton of varieties of meat on giant skewers, and if you want it, They plop it right on your plate! They kept our water refilled, rolls (heavenly and gluten free) stocked up, and they asked if we were looking forward to anything in particular. Then they brought out whatever it was we wanted! Delicious food, super attentive staff, and at the end, when we ordered creme brulee, it came with a birthday greeting on the plate! My friend was super surprised! The dessert was delicious too! If you are celebrating anything, maybe on a date, or just for any reason, I highly recommend it! They just opened up a Walnut Creek location as well! Give them a try, I guarantee you will walk in and roll out!< /review>

<Date>1558448158945</Date>< Text>
We had our mother's day lunch/dinner here and it was well worth the price. The servers have been really helpful on how to go on with getting our fill and the gauchos that served the food have been quick to response. There is about 17 types of Brazilian BBQ that you can pick from and we only went through about 6 or 7. Their lamb chops are great, the flavor or the rosemary combined well with the flavor of the meat. The pork was tender and juicy not dry at all, and the flavor of spices that were used enchances the flavor of the pork just right and their beef was just how I like it (medium to medium rare). I liked how the beef was seasoned just right and how there are some charred parts that made me crave for more. The dessert complimented the BBQ by toning down the experience to end the meal perfectly. My wife, my sister, my daughter and I enjoyed it very much. Next time we will bring our appetite and I may be able to go through all 17 choices in their menu. Thank you for the experience.<//Text>

Excellent Atmosphere...Excellent Food.

One Issue...We visited for a 2pm lunch on a Sunday.  The restaurant wasn't busy at all, but we constantly felt rushed. We drove 2 hours from northern Lake County to visit this restaurant and the whole visit was done in 38 minutes.  When you spend $200 for a meal, you expect to enjoy it and not feel rushed.  There was a constant flow of staff coming to the table to offer food, replace plates, fill water glasses, etc. etc. regardless of our little table cards flipped to the red side. I think its fair to say that 5 minutes never passed without someone visiting the table.

If we make it back to the restaurant, we hope to not feel so rushed.< /review>

My first Brazilian Steakhouse experience and it was amazing. The food is impeccable,  "salad bar" is an understated way to refer to the amazing spread of salads, soups, veggies, cheeses and other amazing items you can get. Salad bar was kept perfectly clean with staff constantly attending it to ensure no messes and everything well-stocked. This is definitely NOT your Souplantation salad bar. Worth every penny you will spend.< /Review>

<username>Amanda Moore<//username><Time>1512709426027< /Time><Rating>5<//Rating>< text>
Great selection of food. Impeccable staff!
You sit down for drinks, then to a salad bar (not much salad, mostly cheeses, deli meat, sun dried tomatoes, olive dishes, sushi, veggie dishes, and 2 bowls of salad).
Upon arrival to your table, you are greated with an onslaught of various meat (chicken pork, salmon, and lamb). You may pass or accept any meat (rare, medium or done, and in between). There's a red and green card to let them know if you want more meat or if you are enjoying the food and don't want another slice at that time. There's one server for a table with 3-4 others serving the meat. It is a we'll trained and choreographed meal.
Once done with the main course, there's dessert too.
Overall great experience, clean restaurant, and gregarious staff.</text>

< text>
The steak here was some of the best I've ever had in my life. There's quite a large selection of meats to choose from, most of which are beef. Each meat item served has its own flavor and texture, which keeps the experience fresh as you try the different items. There's also a salad bar (which has a few other items such as bread, not just salad) that you can use if you need a break from meat during your meal. The atmosphere and service is also great. Just make sure you're hungry before you come, as it's all-you-can-eat and you'll want to get your money's worth, as it's very expensive. For this reason, it's a place that's best visited for special occasions.< /text>

< review>
Always a great experience. Servers are kind, always in a great mood and super accommodating. The meat preparations are en point. All you can eat can be great after a day of tasting heavy wines of Napa.

Don't go if you are looking for a quiet, uninterrupted meal. The nature of this is restaurant is interactive and you should be ready for a steady flow of meat sabers until the check comes. It's a lot of fun if you are ready for a familiar family style dinner and the meat comma that follows.

Kid friendly, if your kids like meat. Loud enough to get away with minor tantrums and servers are understanding- bringing kids cups and removing sharp knives.

Can generally sneak in without a resy, but not always.  Definitely worth a try at least once for the fun of it.</review>

Food was really good! A bit pricey, but then again it is Napa... anywhere you go other than Denny's and fast food is going to be expensive! Food was fantastic, it is an all you can eat place, and they even have cards on the tables for the meat that says yes please on one side,and no thank you on the other! < Review>
ENDLESS (!!) cuts of meat are juicy and delicious, and this place has just enough atmosphere to prove they are serious about the business, without being too good for my kind (nice pair of jeans and collared shirt is ok).  Noise level is befitting of a place full of hungry, excited customers (you may not be able to hear conversation a few seats away). Buffet with a few dozen selections of hors d'oeuvres is complementary, as is a small selection of desserts.  Drinks and other desserts can be purchased in addition.  Be prepared to spend over $75 per person, knowing that in return you will leave with a greater appreciation of the fullness of life.<//Review>

< Review>
Ok, so I don't leave reviews ever, and I mean ever! But to put it simply this place has delivered for me twice in my life. The first time being my 3rd date with the woman I ended up marrying, the 2nd time being my wedding reception. My wife an her family are from Brazil and I wanted to make sure they felt at home. The level of service, quality of food and overall joy throughout the entire experience made it a memorable time. All I can say is show up hungry and ready for meat because even skipping breakfast and lunch, I didn't have enough room for the train of delicious meat. This is authentic Brazilian food and an experience given with love an care. Thanks again to this amazing place.</Review>

<Review>I visited the restaurant with my wife for my birthday dinner over the Thanksgiving holiday weekend.

We were greeted at our table by our waiter JJ. He is Brazilian and was fun to talk with. He gave us the lowdown on how the restaurant worked since it was our first time in a Brazilian steakhouse.

We started at the salad bar which was much more then that. Smoked salmon, vegetables, sushi, cheese and much more. Be careful not to eat much to save room for the main course.

We also had Pao de Queijo which is Brazilian cheese bread. So good but don't fill up.

We were then told to turn over these cards at our table when we were ready to eat. They had red on one side and green in the other for obvious reasons.

We went green and waiter after waiter came by our table to slice of tender goodness of bottom Sirloin, top sirloin, braised rib, lamb chops, filet minion with and without bacon. On and on everything was delicious. Salmon, sausages, ribs all tender and mouth watering. We had to turn over the red card a few times.

After dinner JJ brought out a birthday chocolate molton desert for my wife and I to share. Outstanding.

Overall experience great. Food awesome. You will not leave hungry. On the pricey side but worth it.<//Review>< rating>
5</rating>

<name>AM Young< /name><text>Wow. Too amazing for words yet I will attempt to convey the sheer pleasure as well as satisfaction of experience we had today.
My husband and I arrived early for dinner service ( we left home early not knowing that the restaurant was so easily located right off the freeway with very clear signs) which began promptly at 5pm.
Although we were early by about 15 min we were greeted most generally by the hostess who seated us at a table by the bar with not one but three menus to order a multitude of dishes and cocktails to pass the time.
I went to wash my hands and found that the bathroom was not simply clean but had a scent of flowers. It was similar to a fresh spring bouquet.
I was again amazed by the beautiful fountain that greeted me at the sink. Quite unique in that it resembled an antique wine pump. Truly amazing. I had to ask my husband to "go and wash your hands" because I knew I couldn't describe it and give it the awe inspiring description it deserved.
He loved the attention to detail as well (I also told him I would love that to be an addition to our bathroom remodel).
The restaurant is simply beautiful. Upscale, classy yet without pretense.
A fancy gala or (as we were in) jeans and shorts are all completely comfortable.
As we were greeted and attended to by many staff, one of which took our drink order promptly as well as bringing soft, warm, egg shaped and sized bread in a basket that brought back memories of my mother's home made bread with home made yeast, full of love and flavor. Delicately crispy crust with a warm and tender inside...Mmmmm.
Before I knew it we were being seated. She gave us our choice. Nice touch.
We started at the ample salad bar. Not wanting to fill up on salad as this was our first experience at an all you can eat Brazilian bbq, I limited my choices to the asparagus, cheeses, chicken salad, brown bread and butter. Too delicious!
Then the meats begin to come.
The entire staff is welcoming. Our server kindly explaining the way it all works and how to get more from the menu. The laughter, the quality, the atmosphere, the attention to detail. Every detail. Even when I wanted to save the rack of lamb bones for our dogs (we have three), it was not simply accommodated but done without hesitation.
I ate more than I've ever managed. Ribeye, rack of lamb, sirloin, salmon, filet and more. Most was cooked to perfection. The salmon was dry but saved by a bit of lemon and the sweet yet tart sauce served with it. The end pieces of sirloin my husband had were a bit tough but only in comparison to the melt in your mouth meats the proceeded it.
When one of the meat entrees was not in circulation, I had but to ask and it was moments later on my plate.
I have not had such a euphoric dining experience in over 20 years.
Thank you, thank you, thank you!!!
There are many places with 5 star or close to 5 star ratings. But  we have been disappointed by most. On the other hand... YOU all, truly deserve it! We will be dining again and again. Most importantly we will be singing your praises and bring others to enjoy the pleasure of dining with you!
Thank you for a world class experience at Galpao Goucho in Napa!</text>< response>
None<//response>
